<!-- Replace ß -->
<script type="text/javascript">
    function getTextNodes(element) {
        var node
                , matchedNodes = []
                , walker = document.createTreeWalker(element, NodeFilter.SHOW_ELEMENT, null, false);

        while (node = walker.nextNode()) {
            if(window.getComputedStyle(node).getPropertyValue('text-transform') === 'uppercase') {

                // second & third if included just to make it more transparent what happens here
                if(node.nodeName !== 'svg' || node.nodeName !== 'path' || node.nodeName !== 'style' || node.nodeName !== 'defs') {
                    if (node.textContent.indexOf('ß') > -1) {
                        matchedNodes.push(node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        return matchedNodes;
    }

    function replaceSharpS(domNode) {
        matchedTextNodes = getTextNodes(domNode);

        matchedTextNodes.forEach(function (textNode) {
            var replacedText = textNode.textContent.replace(/ß/gmi, 'ss');
            textNode.textContent = replacedText;
        });

    }

    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        replaceSharpS(document.querySelector('body'));
    }, false);

</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        (function forceSSOLoginWhenNeeded() {
            var getCookie = function (cookie) {
                var cookieName = cookie + "=";
                var cookies = document.cookie.split(';');

                for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
                    var cookieData = cookies[i];

                    while (cookieData.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        cookieData = cookieData.substring(1);
                    }

                    if (cookieData.indexOf(cookieName) == 0) {
                        return cookieData.substring(cookieName.length, cookieData.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            };

            var loginProcess = fcbConfig.connections.loginProcess;
            var cmsCookieExists = !!getCookie(loginProcess.cookieName);
            var ssoCookieExists = !!getCookie(loginProcess.cookieNameGlobal);
            if (!cmsCookieExists && ssoCookieExists) {
                if (loginProcess.loginUrlRedirect !== '') {
                    location.href = loginProcess.loginUrlRedirect;
                }
            }
        })();
    </script>
